                                    Dim1txt:="Dimension Value".Name;


                                  JobTemp.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 1 Code",Job."Global Dimension 1 Code");
                                  JobTemp.SETRANGE("Project Type",Job."Project Type");
                                  IF NOT JobTemp.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
                                    //Avslutade projekt
                                    IF PT.GET(Job."Project Type") THEN BEGIN
                                      //Avslutat aktuellt Ür, ack.
                                      CLEAR(JobClosed2);
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 1 Code",Job."Global Dimension 1 Code");
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Project Status",JobClosed2."Project Status"::Finished);
                                      JobClosed2.SETFILTER("Single/Main/Sub Project",'%1|%2',0,1);
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Project Type",Job."Project Type");
                                      JobClosed2.SETFILTER("Posting Date Closing",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(Period,3)),Period);
                                      IF JobClosed2.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
                                        CLEAR(JLE2);
                                        JLE2.SETRANGE("Main Project No.",JobClosed2."No.");
                                        JLE2.CALCSUMS(JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)",JLE2."Total Price (LCY)");
                                        ClosedNewRev:=ClosedNewRev+(JLE2."Total Price (LCY)"*-1);
                                        ClosedNewCost:=ClosedNewCost+JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)";
                                        JLE2.SETRANGE("Cost Type",JLE2."Cost Type"::Sundry);
                                        JLE2.CALCSUMS(JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)");
                                        ClosedNewCostTim:=ClosedNewCostTim+JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)";
                                      UNTIL JobClosed2.NEXT=0;
                                      ClosedNewCost:=ClosedNewCost-ClosedNewCostTim;
                                      //Avslutat aktuellt Ür - 1M, ack
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 1 Code",Job."Global Dimension 1 Code");
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Project Status",JobClosed2."Project Status"::Finished);
                                      JobClosed2.SETFILTER("Single/Main/Sub Project",'%1..%2',0,1);
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Project Type",Job."Project Type");
                                      JobClosed2.SETFILTER("Posting Date Closing",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),3)),CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));
                                      IF JobClosed2.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
                                        CLEAR(JLE2);
                                        JLE2.SETRANGE("Main Project No.",JobClosed2."No.");
                                        JLE2.CALCSUMS(JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)",JLE2."Total Price (LCY)");
                                        ClosedOldRev:= ClosedOldRev+(JLE2."Total Price (LCY)"*-1);
                                        ClosedOldCost:=ClosedOldCost+JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)";
                                        JLE2.SETRANGE("Cost Type",JLE2."Cost Type"::Sundry);
                                        JLE2.CALCSUMS(JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)");
                                        ClosedOldCostTim:=ClosedOldCostTim+JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)";
                                      UNTIL JobClosed2.NEXT=0;
                                      ClosedOldCost:=ClosedOldCost-ClosedOldCostTim;

                                      JobTemp.INIT;
                                      JobTemp."No.":=Job."No.";
                                      JobTemp.INSERT(FALSE);    //JobTemp.INSERT(TRUE);  IME428
                                      JobTemp."Global Dimension 1 Code":=Job."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                      JobTemp."Project Type":=Job."Project Type";
                                      JobTemp.MODIFY(FALSE);    //JobTemp.MODIFY(TRUE); IME428

                                      //Avslutat aktuellt Ür, tom aktuell mÜnad
                                      CLEAR(JobClosed2);
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 1 Code",Job."Global Dimension 1 Code");
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Project Status",JobClosed2."Project Status"::Finished);
                                      JobClosed2.SETFILTER("Single/Main/Sub Project",'%1|%2',0,1);
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Project Type",Job."Project Type");
                                      JobClosed2.SETFILTER("Posting Date Closing",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(Period,3)),Period);
                                      IF JobClosed2.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
                                        GLEntryWIP.SETFILTER(Description,'WIP Project No. '+JobClosed2."No.");
                                        GLEntryWIP.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.",'%1..','3000');
                                        GLEntryWIP.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(Period,3)),Period);
                                        GLEntryWIP.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                        WIPActYearClosed:= WIPActYearClosed+(GLEntryWIP.Amount*-1);

                                        GLEntryWIP.SETFILTER(Description,'LR Project No. '+JobClosed2."No.");
                                        GLEntryWIP.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                        LRActYearClosed:= LRActYearClosed+GLEntryWIP.Amount;

                                        CLEAR(JLE2);
                                        JLE2.SETRANGE("Main Project No.",JobClosed2."No.");
                                        JLE2.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(Period,3)),Period);
                                        JLE2.CALCSUMS(JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)",JLE2."Total Price (LCY)");
                                        ClosedPreRes2014Turn:=ClosedPreRes2014Turn+((JLE2."Total Price (LCY)"*-1)+(WIPActYearClosed));
                                        ClosedPreRes2014:=ClosedPreRes2014+(((JLE2."Total Price (LCY)"*-1)+(WIPActYearClosed)) - (JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)"+(LRActYearClosed)));
                                      UNTIL JobClosed2.NEXT=0;

                                      //Avslutat aktuellt Ür, tom fîregÜende mÜnad
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Global Dimension 1 Code",Job."Global Dimension 1 Code");
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Project Status",JobClosed2."Project Status"::Finished);
                                      JobClosed2.SETFILTER("Single/Main/Sub Project",'%1..%2',0,1);
                                      JobClosed2.SETRANGE("Project Type",Job."Project Type");
                                      JobClosed2.SETFILTER("Posting Date Closing",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),3)),CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));
                                      IF JobClosed2.FINDSET THEN REPEAT
                                        GLEntryWIP.SETFILTER(Description,'WIP Project No. '+JobClosed2."No.");
                                        GLEntryWIP.SETFILTER("G/L Account No.",'%1..','3000');
                                        GLEntryWIP.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),3)),CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));
                                        GLEntryWIP.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                        WIPActYearClosedOld:= WIPActYearClosedOld+(GLEntryWIP.Amount*-1);

                                        GLEntryWIP.SETFILTER(Description,'LR Project No. '+JobClosed2."No.");
                                        GLEntryWIP.CALCSUMS(Amount);
                                        LRActYearClosedOld:= LRActYearClosedOld+GLEntryWIP.Amount;

                                        CLEAR(JLE2);
                                        JLE2.SETRANGE("Main Project No.",JobClosed2."No.");
                                        JLE2.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,1,DATE2DMY(CALCDATE('-1M',Period),3)),CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));
                                        JLE2.CALCSUMS(JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)",JLE2."Total Price (LCY)");
                                        ClosedPreRes2014OldTurn:=ClosedPreRes2014OldTurn+((JLE2."Total Price (LCY)"*-1)+(WIPActYearClosedOld));
                                        ClosedPreRes2014Old:=ClosedPreRes2014Old+(((JLE2."Total Price (LCY)"*-1)+(WIPActYearClosedOld)) - (JLE2."Total Cost (LCY)"+(LRActYearClosedOld)));
                                      UNTIL JobClosed2.NEXT=0;

                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  //>> 160211 ITERO.SB
                                  //Fakturerad intÑkt aktuell period
                                  JLE4.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',DMY2DATE(1,DATE2DMY(Period,2),DATE2DMY(Period,3)),CALCDATE('<CM>',Period));
                                  JLE4.SETRANGE("Main Project No.",Job."No.");
                                  JLE4.SETRANGE("Cost Type",JLE4."Cost Type"::Revenues);
                                  JLE4.CALCSUMS("Total Price (LCY)");
                                  InvPeriod:=JLE4."Total Price (LCY)"*-1;

                                  //Fakturerad intÑkt fîregÜende period
                                  JLE4.SETFILTER("Posting Date",'%1..%2',CALCDATE('-1M',
                                  DMY2DATE(1,DATE2DMY(Period,2),DATE2DMY(Period,3))),CALCDATE('<CM>',CALCDATE('-1M',Period)));
                                  JLE4.CALCSUMS("Total Price (LCY)");
                                  InvPeriodPrev:=JLE4."Total Price (LCY)"*-1;

                                  LR:=LR*-1;
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Project Type,Bill-to Customer No.,Contract Type,Project Status,Single/Main/Sub Project }

    { 1100285503;1;Column;JobNo              ;
               SourceExpr=Job."No." }

                               DimensionCode := Dimension.Code;
                             RequestOptionsPage.UPDATE;
                           END;
                            }

      { 1100285501;1;Field  ;
                  CaptionML=[ENU=Dimension Value;
                             NOR=Dimensjonsverdi;

                           BEGIN
                             DimensionValue.SETRANGE("Dimension Code", DimensionCode);
                             IF PAGE.RUNMODAL(0, DimensionValue) = ACTION::LookupOK THEN
                               DimensionValueCode := DimensionValue.Code;
                             RequestOptionsPage.UPDATE;
                           END;
                            }

      JobClosed2@1000000017 : Record 11072003;
      WIPActYearClosed@1000000016 : Decimal;
      LRActYearClosed@1000000015 : Decimal;
      WIPActYearClosedOld@1000000014 : Decimal;
      LRActYearClosedOld@1000000013 : Decimal;
      WIPActYearBal@1000000031 : Decimal;
      LRActYearBal@1000000032 : Decimal;
      TilfDate@1000000033 : Date;
      Date1@1000000039 : Date;
      Date2@1000000038 : Date;
      Date3@1000000037 : Date;
      Date4@1000000036 : Date;
      WIPPeriod2@1000000035 : Decimal;
      LRPeriod2@1000000034 : Decimal;

    PROCEDURE GetProject@1100285500();
    BEGIN
      CLEAR(ProjPreclResultRec);
      ResultType:=ResultType::Preclosure;
      PostingDate:=Period;
      AddNew:=TRUE;

      IF Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD" = Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD"::No THEN
        EXIT;

      IF (Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD" = Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD"::"Preclosure Result") AND
         (ResultType = ResultType::Provision) THEN
        EXIT;

      IF (Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD" = Job."Allow Precl. R./Prov. Loss OLD"::"Provision Loss") AND
         (ResultType = ResultType::Preclosure) THEN
        EXIT;

      ProjPreclResultRec.RESET;
      ProjPreclResultRec.SETCURRENTKEY("Project No.","Line No.");
      ProjPreclResultRec.SETRANGE("Project No.", Job."No.");
      LineNo := 10000;  //Select new lineno.
      IF ProjPreclResultRec.FINDLAST THEN
        LineNo := ProjPreclResultRec."Line No." + 10000;

      ProjPreclResultRec.RESET;
      ProjPreclResultRec.SETCURRENTKEY("Project No.","Posting Date","Line No.");
      ProjPreclResultRec.SETRANGE("Project No.",Job."No.");
      //ProjPreclResultRec.SETFILTER("Posting Date", '>%1', PostingDate);
      //IF ProjPreclResultRec.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN   //Only when there are not entries with newer posting dates
      //  ProjPreclResultRec.SETRANGE("Posting Date", PostingDate);
      //  ProjPreclResultRec.SETRANGE(Posted, FALSE);
      //  IF ProjPreclResultRec.ISEMPTY THEN BEGIN   //Only when there are no entries on posting date which are not posted
      //    ProjPreclResultRec.SETRANGE(Posted, TRUE);
      //    IF ProjPreclResultRec.ISEMPTY OR AddNew THEN BEGIN
            ProjPreclResultRec.RESET;

            IF ResultType = ResultType::Provision THEN
              IF ProjPreclResultRec.CheckPreclResultPresent011(FALSE) THEN
                EXIT;
                //CurrReport.SKIP;

            ProjPreclResultRec.INIT; //** Call C010248
            ProjPreclResultRec."Project No.":= Job."No.";
            ProjPreclResultRec.VALIDATE("Line No.", LineNo);
            ProjPreclResultRec."Posting Date":= PostingDate;
            ProjPreclResultRec."Result Type" := ResultType;
            ProjPreclResultRec."Prognosis Level" := Job."Prognosis Level"; //C000501

            IF ProjPreclResultRec.INSERT(TRUE) THEN
              Ok:=TRUE;

      //    END;
      //  END;
      //END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateResult@1100525001(VAR IProjPreclResultRec@1100525002 : TEMPORARY Record 11012093;IProjRecordingLine@1100525004 : Record 11072021;ICalledFromProjectRecording@1100525003 : Boolean);
    VAR
      lvDampingRatioRec@1100525001 : Record 11072019;
      lvHoldPreclRec@1100525006 : TEMPORARY Record 11012093;
      lvPrognRevenuePresent@1100525000 : Boolean;
      lvPrognRevenue@1100525007 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      WITH IProjPreclResultRec DO BEGIN
        JobSetup.GET; //Function can be called from outside
        TESTFIELD(Posted, FALSE);
        lvHoldPreclRec := IProjPreclResultRec;
        INIT; //Clear previous calculations and other progress fields
        "Result Type" := lvHoldPreclRec."Result Type";
        "Global Dimension 1 Code" := lvHoldPreclRec."Global Dimension 1 Code";

        JobRec.GET("Project No.");
        JobRec.SETFILTER("Cumulation Filter", '..%1', "Posting Date");
        JobRec.SETRANGE("Period Filter", "Posting Date");

        DetermineProgressDate.DetermineBothDates(JobRec,FALSE);
        DeterminePrognosisDate.DetermineBothDates(JobRec);

        JobRec.FillProjectFilter(ProjFilter);
        JobRec.SETFILTER("Project Filter", ProjFilter);
        JobRec.CALCFIELDS(
          "Actual Costs",
          "Project Contract Amount",
          "Extension Contract Amount",
          "Options Contract Amount");

        CLEAR(PrognosisRec);
        "Prognosis Total Cost" := 0;
        IF JobSetup."Purch. Result in Precl. Result" THEN
          "Purchase Result" := CostContMgt.PurchResultProject(JobRec, TRUE);
        "Prognosis Total Revenues" := 0;
        "Prognosis Financial Result" := 0;
        IF JobRec.GETFILTER("Prognosis Filter") <> '' THEN BEGIN
          PrognosisRec.SETRANGE("Project No.", "Project No.");
          PrognosisRec.SETFILTER("Prognosis Date", JobRec.GETFILTER("Prognosis Filter"));
          IF PrognosisRec.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
            IF PrognosisRec."Prognosis Level" = PrognosisRec."Prognosis Level"::Rough THEN BEGIN
              "Prognosis Total Cost" := PrognosisRec."Rough Prognosis Total Cost";
              "Prognosis Total Revenues" := PrognosisRec."Rough Prognosis Total Revenues";
              lvPrognRevenuePresent := "Prognosis Total Revenues" <> 0;
      //>>4PS-002
            //END ELSE BEGIN
            END ELSE
              IF JobRec."Forecast Level" = JobRec."Forecast Level"::"Cost Component" THEN BEGIN
                PrognosisRec.CALCFIELDS("Prognosis Total Revenue CC", "Prognosis Total Cost CC");
                "Prognosis Total Cost" := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Total Cost CC";
                "Prognosis Total Revenues" := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Total Revenue CC";// + PrognosisRec."Project Invoiced";
                "Purchase Result" := 0;
                //>> 140514 ITERO.SB IME-145
                PrognosisRec.CALCFIELDS("Prognosis Revenue CC");
                //<<
                lvPrognRevenuePresent := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Revenue CC" <> 0;
              END ELSE
      //>>4PS-002
            BEGIN
              PrognosisRec.CALCFIELDS("Prognosis Revenue", "Prognosis Total Cost");
              "Prognosis Total Cost" := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Total Cost";
              "Prognosis Total Revenues" := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Revenue" + PrognosisRec."Project Invoiced";
              lvPrognRevenuePresent := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Revenue" <> 0;
            END;
            "Prognosis Financial Result" := "Prognosis Total Revenues" - ("Prognosis Total Cost" + "Purchase Result") ;
          END;
        END;
        "Actual Cost" := JobRec."Actual Costs" ;
        "Contract Amount" :=
          JobRec."Project Contract Amount" +
          JobRec."Extension Contract Amount" +
          JobRec."Options Contract Amount";

        //IF lvPrognRevenuePresent THEN
          lvPrognRevenue := "Prognosis Total Revenues";
        //ELSE
        //  lvPrognRevenue := "Contract Amount";

        IF ICalledFromProjectRecording THEN
          PrognEndResVersusContractPr := IProjRecordingLine."Progn. End Res. Vs. Contract"
        ELSE BEGIN
          PrognEndResVersusContractPr := CostContMgt.PrognEndResVrsContrAmtProject(JobRec, TRUE);
        END;
        IF lvPrognRevenuePresent THEN
          PrognEndResVersusContractPr := PrognEndResVersusContractPr - "Contract Amount" + "Prognosis Total Revenues";

        CALCFIELDS("Previous Actual Precl. Result", "Prev. Actual Preclosure Rev.", "Prev. Actual Preclosure Cost");

        "Progress % Base" := 0;

        CASE JobRec."Preclosure Result" OF
          JobRec."Preclosure Result"::Allowed,
          JobRec."Preclosure Result"::"Sales Allowed":
            IF ICalledFromProjectRecording THEN
              "Progress % Base" := IProjRecordingLine.Progress
            ELSE
              "Progress % Base" := CostContMgt.AllowedPercProject(JobRec,TRUE);
          JobRec."Preclosure Result"::Invoiced: //08-07-09
            BEGIN
              JobRec.CALCFIELDS(Revenues);
      //M C-027051 so
      //        IF JobRec."Project Contract Amount" + JobRec."Extension Contract Amount" + JobRec."Options Contract Amount" <> 0 THEN
      //          "Progress % Base" :=
      //            JobRec.Revenues /
      //            (JobRec."Project Contract Amount" + JobRec."Extension Contract Amount" + JobRec."Options Contract Amount") * 100
      //M C-027051 sn
              IF lvPrognRevenue <> 0 THEN
                "Progress % Base" := (JobRec.Revenues / lvPrognRevenue) * 100;
      //M C-027051 en
            END;
          ELSE
            IF JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress" = JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress"::"Cost to Revenue" THEN BEGIN
              IF lvPrognRevenue <> 0 THEN
                "Progress % Base" :=  ("Actual Cost"/lvPrognRevenue) * 100;
            END;
            IF JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress" = JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress"::"Cost to Cost" THEN BEGIN
              IF (lvPrognRevenue - PrognEndResVersusContractPr <> 0) THEN
                "Progress % Base" := ("Actual Cost"/(lvPrognRevenue-PrognEndResVersusContractPr)) * 100;
            END;
            //C-026777.sn
            IF JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress" = JobSetup."Method Proj. Progress"::"Cost to Cost (incl. Firm Commitments)" THEN BEGIN
              IF (lvPrognRevenue - PrognEndResVersusContractPr <> 0) THEN BEGIN
                JobRec.CALCFIELDS("Received/Not Invoiced", "Open Ovh. Surch. Firm (Purch.)");  // C-026777
                FirmCommitments := JobRec."Received/Not Invoiced" + JobRec."Open Ovh. Surch. Firm (Purch.)";  // C-026777
                "Progress % Base" := (("Actual Cost" + FirmCommitments)/(lvPrognRevenue-PrognEndResVersusContractPr)) * 100;
              END;
            END;
            //C-026777.en
        END;

        IF (JobRec."Preclosure Result" = JobRec."Preclosure Result"::"Sales Progress") OR
           (JobRec."Preclosure Result" = JobRec."Preclosure Result"::"Sales Allowed") THEN BEGIN

          IF gvCountUnits THEN BEGIN
            PlotRec.RESET;
            PlotRec.SETRANGE("Project No.", JobRec."No.");
            "Units Saleable" := PlotRec.COUNT;
            PlotRec.SETFILTER("Sales Status", '%1..', PlotRec."Sales Status"::Sold);
            PlotRec.SETFILTER("Sales Status Since", '..%1', "Posting Date");
            "Units Sold" := PlotRec.COUNT;
          END;

          IF "Units Saleable" <> 0 THEN
            "Sales Progress" := ROUND(100 * "Units Sold" / "Units Saleable")
          ELSE
            "Sales Progress" := 0;
          "Progress %" := ROUND("Progress % Base" * ("Sales Progress" / 100));
        END ELSE
          "Progress %" := "Progress % Base";

      //>>4PS-002
        IF JobRec."Forecast Level" = JobRec."Forecast Level"::"Cost Component" THEN BEGIN
          "Progress % Base" := 0;
          IF "Prognosis Total Cost" <> 0 THEN
            "Progress % Base" := (JobRec."Actual Costs" / "Prognosis Total Cost" * 100);
          "Progress %" := "Progress % Base";
        END;
      //>>4PS-002

      //>> 150604 ITERO.SB IME-366 Change calculation of Progress for cost object level
        IF JobRec."Forecast Level" = JobRec."Forecast Level"::"Cost Object" THEN BEGIN
          "Progress % Base" := 0;
          IF "Prognosis Total Cost" <> 0 THEN
            "Progress % Base" := (JobRec."Actual Costs" / "Prognosis Total Cost" * 100);
          "Progress %" := "Progress % Base";
        END;
      //<<

        IF "Progress %" > 100 THEN  //M16746
          "Progress %" := 100;      //M16746

        //>> 150608 ITERO.SB IME-366 Change calculation of Progress
        IF "Progress %" < 0 THEN BEGIN
          IF ("Prognosis Total Cost" > 0) AND (JobRec."Actual Costs" < 0) THEN
            "Progress %" := 0;
        END;

        IF "Progress %" < 0 THEN BEGIN
          IF ("Prognosis Total Cost" < 0) AND (JobRec."Actual Costs" > 0) THEN
            "Progress %" := 0;
        END;
        //>>


        IF "Result Type" = "Result Type"::"Preclosure Result" THEN BEGIN
          "Expected Final Result" := "Prognosis Financial Result";
          "Corrected Final Result":= "Expected Final Result";
          "Calculated Turnover" := ROUND("Progress %" * lvPrognRevenue / 100);
          "Actual Preclosure Revenue" := "Calculated Turnover" - "Prev. Actual Preclosure Rev.";

          IF "Expected Final Result" < 0 THEN
            "Calculated Preclosure Result" := "Expected Final Result"
          ELSE BEGIN
            "Calculated Preclosure Result" := "Progress %" * "Expected Final Result" / 100 ;
            lvDampingRatioRec.SETFILTER("Until Production", '>=%1', ROUND("Progress %", 1, '>'));
            IF lvDampingRatioRec.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
              "Calculated Preclosure Result" := "Progress %" * lvDampingRatioRec.Ratio * "Expected Final Result" / 100;
            END;
          END;

          "Calculated Preclosure Result" := ROUND("Calculated Preclosure Result");
          "Corrected Preclosure Result" := "Calculated Preclosure Result" ;
          "Actual Preclosure Result" := "Calculated Preclosure Result" - "Previous Actual Precl. Result";
          "Actual Preclosure Result" := ROUND("Actual Preclosure Result");

          "Calculated Cost" := ROUND("Calculated Turnover" - "Calculated Preclosure Result");
          "Corrected Preclosure Cost" := "Calculated Cost";
          "Actual Preclosure Cost" := ROUND("Corrected Preclosure Cost" - "Prev. Actual Preclosure Cost");
          "Progress % Actual" := "Progress %";  //C001798.n
        END ELSE BEGIN
          "Progress % Actual" := 0;  //C001798.n
          IF "Prognosis Financial Result" < 0 THEN
            "Calculated Provision" := "Prognosis Financial Result"
          ELSE
            "Calculated Provision" := 0;

          CALCFIELDS("Previous Actual Provision");
          "Actual Provision" := "Calculated Provision" - "Previous Actual Provision"
        END;

        "Prognosis Date" := JobRec.GETRANGEMAX("Prognosis Filter");
        "Progress Date" := JobRec.GETRANGEMAX("Progress Filter");
        "Prognosis Level" := PrognosisRec."Prognosis Level";
        MODIFY;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalculateWIP@1100285100(JobLoc@1100285102 : Record 11072003;Period@1100285109 : Date);
    VAR
      gPrognosis@1100285100 : Record 11012034;
      prognosisFound@1100285101 : Boolean;
      JobActualCosts@1100285106 : Decimal;
      JobOpenAmountHours@1100285105 : Decimal;
      JobOpenOvhSurchHours@1100285104 : Decimal;
      JobInvoicedPrice@1100285103 : Decimal;
      JobSub@1100285107 : Record 11072003;
      prognFinResult@1100285108 : Decimal;
      pct@1100285111 : Decimal;
      JobActCosts@1100285112 : Decimal;
    BEGIN

      gPrognosis.SETRANGE("Project No.",JobLoc."No.");
      gPrognosis.SETRANGE("Prognosis Date",0D,CALCDATE('<CM>',Period));//selectedDate);
      prognosisFound := gPrognosis.FINDLAST;


      JobLoc.SETFILTER("Wage Component Type Filter",'<>%1',JobLoc."Wage Component Type Filter"::"Expense hours");
      //>>170207 ITERO.SB
      JobLoc.SETRANGE("Cumulation Filter",0D,CALCDATE('<CM>',Period));//selectedDate);  //170206
      //<<
      JobLoc.CALCFIELDS("Actual Costs","Open Amount (Hours)","Open Ovh. Surch. (Hours)","Invoiced Price");

      JobActualCosts := JobLoc."Actual Costs";
      JobOpenAmountHours := JobLoc."Open Amount (Hours)";
      JobOpenOvhSurchHours := JobLoc."Open Ovh. Surch. (Hours)";
      JobInvoicedPrice := JobLoc."Invoiced Price";

      IF JobLoc."Single/Main/Sub Project" = JobLoc."Single/Main/Sub Project"::"Main Project" THEN BEGIN
        JobSub.SETRANGE("Cumulation Filter",0D,CALCDATE('<CM>',Period));//selectedDate);  //170207
        JobSub.SETFILTER("No.",'<>%1',JobLoc."No.");
        JobSub.SETRANGE("Main Project",JobLoc."Main Project");
        IF JobSub.FINDSET(FALSE) THEN
        REPEAT
          JobSub.CALCFIELDS("Invoiced Price");
          JobInvoicedPrice += JobSub."Invoiced Price";
        UNTIL JobSub.NEXT=0;
      END;


      IF (JobLoc."Forecast Level" = JobLoc."Forecast Level"::"Cost Component") THEN BEGIN
        gPrognosis.CALCFIELDS("Prognosis Total Cost CC","Prognosis Total Revenue CC");
        IF prognosisFound THEN
          prognosisFound := gPrognosis."Prognosis Total Cost CC" <> 0;
        prognFinResult := (gPrognosis."Prognosis Total Revenue CC" - gPrognosis."Prognosis Total Cost CC");
      END
      ELSE BEGIN
        gPrognosis.CALCFIELDS("Prognosis Total Cost",gPrognosis."Prognosis Revenue");
        IF prognosisFound THEN
          prognosisFound := gPrognosis."Prognosis Total Cost" <> 0;
        prognFinResult := (gPrognosis."Prognosis Revenue" - gPrognosis."Prognosis Total Cost");
      END;

      pct :=0;
      IF prognosisFound THEN
      BEGIN
      //161230
        //JobActCosts := JobActualCosts + JobOpenAmountHours + JobOpenOvhSurchHours;
        JobActCosts := JobActualCosts ;
      //161230

        IF (JobLoc."Forecast Level" = JobLoc."Forecast Level"::"Cost Component") THEN
          pct := JobActCosts / gPrognosis."Prognosis Total Cost CC"
        ELSE
          pct := JobActCosts / gPrognosis."Prognosis Total Cost";
      END;

      //>>170202, re-eanble
      //161227
      IF pct > 1 THEN pct := 1;
      //<<

      IF (JobLoc."Forecast Level" = JobLoc."Forecast Level"::"Cost Component") THEN
        partTotRev := gPrognosis."Prognosis Total Revenue CC" * pct
      ELSE
        partTotRev := gPrognosis."Prognosis Revenue" * pct;

      AmntWip := (JobInvoicedPrice - partTotRev)*-1;

      //IF ROUND(AmntWip,0.01) <> 0 THEN
      //  createGLlines(-AmntWip,AccCredWIP,AccDebWIP,PLAccWIP,
      //                'WIP%1-'+FORMAT(selectedDate,0,'<Year4>-<Month,2>'),'WIP Project No. '+Job."No.");

      //161227
      IF pct > 1 THEN pct := 1;

      //loss-risk
      partTotRev := prognFinResult * ( 1 - pct);
      //IF ROUND(prognFinResult,0.01) < 0 THEN
      //  createGLlines(-partTotRev,PLAccLossRisk,PLAccLossRisk,BalAccLossRisk,
      //                'LR%1-'+FORMAT(selectedDate,0,'<Year4>-<Month,2>'),'LR Project No. '+Job."No."
      //                );


      IF ROUND(prognFinResult,0.01) > 0 THEN
        partTotRev := 0;

      IF ROUND(AmntWip,0.01) = 0 THEN
        AmntWip := 0;
    END;

    BEGIN
    {
      180209 ITERO.SB RFC-257 Created new report (Copy of 81677 PULS-2-NO) + added new columns
      190426 ORANGO.SB IME-1192 PULS3 Fix
      200128 IME-1277 #27331 PULS-NO Sum fix
    }
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
